Source Code

These source-code files were from the printout at the MIT Museum, with many thanks to Deborah Douglas, the Museum's Curator of Science and Technology, for releasing it to us. The printout was digitally photographed by Paul Fjeld. A team of volunteers transcribed the source code manually from these images or, where appropriate, modified already-transcribed but similar source Luminary 131 (Apollo 13) source code to agree with the images from the printout. Note that the page images presented online are of reduced quality, and that higher-quality images are available. Report any conversion errors or legibility problems in page images to info@sandroid.org. Notations on the program listing read, in part:

	GAP:  ASSEMBLE REVISION 001 OF AGC PROGRAM LMY99 BY NASA 2021112-061
	20'35 OCT. 28,1968
Note that the date is the date of the printout, not the date of the program revision.

021087,000015:                                                                                                  ##              2009-06-07 RSB  Fixed a misprint.

021109,000037:                                                                                                  #  RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM 20
021110,000038: 
021111,000039:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021112,000040: 
021113,000041:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO -- 2
021114,000042:                                                                                                  #        BY P. VOLANTE
021115,000043: 
021116,000044:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021117,000045: 
021118,000046:                                                                                                  #        THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO CONTROL THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR FROM
021119,000047:                                                                                                  #        STARTUP THROUGH ACQUISITION AND LOCKON TO THE CSM AND TO UPDATE EITHER 
021120,000048:                                                                                                  #        THE LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (AS SPECIFIED BY THE ASTRONAUT BY DSKY ENTRY)
021121,000049:                                                                                                  #        ON THE BASIS OF THE RR TRACKING DATA.
021122,000050: 
021123,000051:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE --
021124,000052: 
021125,000053:                                                                                                  #        ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E20E
021126,000054: 
021127,000055:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
021128,000056: 
021129,000057:                                                                                                  #        R02BOTH (IMU STATUS CHECK)                      FLAGUP
021130,000058:                                                                                                  #        GOFLASH (PINBALL-DISPLAY)                       FLAGDOWN
021131,000059:                                                                                                  #        R23LEM  (MANUAL ACQUISITION)                    BANKCALL
021132,000060:                                                                                                  #        LS201   (LOS DETERMINATION)                     TASKOVER
021133,000061:                                                                                                  #        LS202   (RANGE LIMIT TEST)
021134,000062:                                                                                                  #        R61LEM  (PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE)
021135,000063:                                                                                                  #        R21LEM  (RR DESIGNATE)                          ENDOFJOB
021136,000064:                                                                                                  #        R22LEM  (DATA READ)                             GOPERF1
021137,000065:                                                                                                  #        R31LEM  (RENDEZVOUS PARAMETER DISPLAY)  
021138,000066:                                                                                                  #        PRIOLARM (PRIORITY DISPLAY)
021139,000067: 
021140,000068:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES --
021141,000069: 
021142,000070:                                                                                                  #        P20 MAY BE TERMINATED IN TWO WAYS -- ASTRONAUT SELECTION OF IDLING
021143,000071:                                                                                                  #        PROGRAM (P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E
021144,000072: 
021145,000073:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES --
021146,000074: 
021147,000075:                                                                                                  #        RANGE GREATER THAN 400 NM DISPLAY
021148,000076: 
021149,000077:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
021150,000078: 
021151,000079:                                                                                                  #        TRKMKCNT = NO OF RENDEZVOUS TRACKING MARKS TAKEN (COUNTER)
021152,000080: 
021153,000081:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
021154,000082: 
021155,000083:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
021156,000084: 
021157,000085:                                                                                                  #        SRCHOPT, RNDVZFLG, ACMODFLG, VEHUPFLG, UPDATFLG, TRACKFLG
021158,000086: 
021159,000087:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
021160,000088: 
021161,000089:                                                                                                  #        CENTRALS -- A,Q,L
021162,000090: 
021163,000091: 25,2062  30,2000                                  SBANK=   LOWSUPER                              #  FOR LOW 2CADR'S.
021164,000092: 
021165,000093: 33,2045                                           BANK     33                                    
021166,000094: 24,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S                                  
021167,000095: 24,2000                                           BANK                                           
021168,000096: 
021169,000097: 24,2000  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
021170,000098: 24,2000                                           COUNT*   $$/P20                                
021171,000099: 24,2000  24,2000               PROG22             =        PROG20

021578,000506:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021579,000507: 
021580,000508:                                                                                                  #        PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE PROGRAM P25
021581,000509:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO -- 3
021582,000510:                                                                                                  #        BY P. VOLANTE
021583,000511: 
021584,000512:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021585,000513: 
021586,000514:                                                                                                  #        THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO COMPUTE THE PREFERRED TRACKING
021587,000515:                                                                                                  #        ATTITUDE OF THE LM TO CONTINUOUSLY POINT THE LM TRTACKING BEACON AT THE
021588,000516:                                                                                                  #        CSM AND TO PERFORM THE MANEUVER TO THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE AND
021589,000517:                                                                                                  #        CONTINUOUSLY MAINTAIN THIS ATTITUDE WITHIN PRESCRIBED LIMITS.
021590,000518: 
021591,000519:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE --
021592,000520: 
021593,000521:                                                                                                  #        ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E25E
021594,000522: 
021595,000523:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED --

021667,000595:                                                                                                  #  DATA READ ROUTINE 22 (LEM)
021668,000596:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021669,000597: 
021670,000598:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO -- 2
021671,000599:                                                                                                  #        BY P. VOLANTE
021672,000600: 
021673,000601:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021674,000602: 
021675,000603:                                                                                                  #        TO PROCESS AUTOMATIC RR MARK DATA TO UPDATE THE STATE VECTOR OF EITHER
021676,000604:                                                                                                  #        LM OR CSM AS DEFINED IN THE RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM (P20)
021677,000605: 
021678,000606:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE --
021679,000607: 
021680,000608:                                                                                                  #        TC      BANKCALL
021681,000609:                                                                                                  #        CADR    R22LEM
021682,000610: 
021683,000611:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED --
021684,000612: 
021685,000613:                                                                                                  #        LSR22.1         GOFLASH         WAITLIST
021686,000614:                                                                                                  #        LSR22.2         PRIOLARM        BANKCALL
021687,000615:                                                                                                  #        LSR22.3         R61LEM
021688,000616: 
021689,000617:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES --

021882,000810:                                                                                                  #  RR DESIGNATE ROUTINE (R21LEM)
021883,000811:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021884,000812: 
021885,000813:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO -- 2
021886,000814:                                                                                                  #        BY P. VOLANTE
021887,000815: 
021888,000816:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021889,000817: 
021890,000818:                                                                                                  #        TO POINT THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR AT THE CSM UNTIL AUTOMATIC ACQUISITION
021891,000819:                                                                                                  #        OF THE CSM IS ACCOMPLISHED BY THE RADAR.  ROUTINE IS CALLED BY P20.
021892,000820: 
021893,000821:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE --
021894,000822: 
021895,000823:                                                                                                  #        TC      BANKCALL
021896,000824:                                                                                                  #        CADR    R21LEM
021897,000825: 
021898,000826:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED --
021899,000827: 
021900,000828:                                                                                                  #        FINDVAC         FLAGUP          ENDOFJOB        PRIOLARM
021901,000829:                                                                                                  #        NOVAC           INTPRET         LPS20.1         PHASCHNG
021902,000830:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST        JOBSLEEP        JOBWAKE         FLAGDOWN
021903,000831:                                                                                                  #        TASKOVER        BANKCALL        RADSTALL        RRDESSM
021904,000832: 
021905,000833:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES
021906,000834:                                                                                                  #        
021907,000835:                                                                                                  #        WHEN LOCK-ON IS ACHIEVED, BRANCH WILL BE TO P20 WHERE R22 (DATA READ
021908,000836:                                                                                                  #        WILL BE SELECTED OR A NEED FOR A MANEUVER (BRANCH TO P20LEMA)
021909,000837: 
021910,000838:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES --
021911,000839: 
021912,000840:                                                                                                  #        PRIORITY ALARM 503 WHEN LOCK-ON HASN'T BEEN ACHIEVED AFTER 30SECS --
021913,000841:                                                                                                  #        THIS REQUIRES ASTRONAUT INTERFACE: SELECTION OF SEARCH OPTION OF
021914,000842:                                                                                                  #        ACQUISITION
021915,000843: 
021916,000844:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
021917,000845: 
021918,000846:                                                                                                  #        SEE LPS20.1, RRDESSM
021919,000847: 
021920,000848:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
021921,000849: 
021922,000850:                                                                                                  #        RRTARGET, RADMODES ARE USED BY LPS20.1 AND RRDESSM
021923,000851: 
021924,000852:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
021925,000853: 
021926,000854:                                                                                                  #        LOSCMFLG        LOKONSW
021927,000855: 
021928,000856:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
021929,000857: 
021930,000858:                                                                                                  #        SEE LPS20.1, RRSESSM

021935,000863: 24,2675           00006                           EXTEND

022107,001035:                                                                                                  #  MANUAL ACQUISITION ROUTINE R23LEM
022108,001036:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022109,001037: 
022110,001038:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO -- 2
022111,001039:                                                                                                  #        BY P. VOLANTE
022112,001040: 
022113,001041:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022114,001042: 
022115,001043:                                                                                                  #        TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY MANUAL OPERATION OF THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
022116,001044: 
022117,001045:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE --
022118,001046: 
022119,001047:                                                                                                  #        TC      R23LEM
022120,001048: 
022121,001049:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
022122,001050: 
022123,001051:                                                                                                  #        BANKCALL        R61LEM
022124,001052:                                                                                                  #        SETMINDB        GOPERF1
022125,001053: 
022126,001054:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES --
022127,001055: 
022128,001056:                                                                                                  #        IN RESPONSE TO THE GOPERF1,     SELECTION OF ENTER WILL RECYCLE R23
022129,001057:                                                                                                  #                                        SELECTION OF PROC WILL CONTINUE R23
022130,001058:                                                                                                  #                                        SELECTION OF TERM WILL TERMINATE R23 + P20
022131,001059: 
022132,001060:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES --
022133,001061:

022135,001063: 
022136,001064:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
022137,001065: 
022138,001066:                                                                                                  #        N.A.
022139,001067: 
022140,001068:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED --

022191,001119:                                                                                                  #  SEARCH ROUTINE R24LEM
022192,001120:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022193,001121: 
022194,001122:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO -- 2
022195,001123:                                                                                                  #        BY P. VOLANTE
022196,001124: 
022197,001125:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022198,001126: 
022199,001127:                                                                                                  #        TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY A SEARCH PATTERN WHEN THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR HAS
022200,001128:                                                                                                  #        FAILED TO ACQUIRE TEH CSM IN THE AUTOMATIC TRACKING MODE AND TO ALLOW
022201,001129:                                                                                                  #        THE ASTRONAUT TO CONFIRM THAT REACQUISITION HAS NOT BEEN IN SIDELOBE.
022202,001130: 
022203,001131:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
022204,001132: 
022205,001133:                                                                                                  #        CAF     PRIONN
022206,001134:                                                                                                  #        TC      FINDVAC
022207,001135:                                                                                                  #        EBANK=  DATAGOOD
022208,001136:                                                                                                  #        2CADR   R24LEM
022209,001137: 
022210,001138:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
022211,001139: 
022212,001140:                                                                                                  #        FLAGUP          FLAGDOWN        BANKCALL
022213,001141:                                                                                                  #        R61LEM          GOFLASHR        FINDVAC
022214,001142:                                                                                                  #        ENDOFJOB        NOVAC           LSR24.1
022215,001143: 
022216,001144:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES --
022217,001145: 
022218,001146:                                                                                                  #        ASTRONAUT RESPONSE TO DISPLAY OF OMEGA AND DATAGOOD.  HE CAN EITHER
022219,001147:                                                                                                  #        REJECT BY TERMINATING (SEARCH OPTION AND RESELECTING P20) OR ACCEPT BY
022220,001148:                                                                                                  #        PROCEEDING (EXIT ROUTINE AND RETURN TO AUTO MODE IN P20)
022221,001149: 
022222,001150:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES --
022223,001151: 
022224,001152:                                                                                                  #        SEE NORMAL EXIT MODES ABOVE
022225,001153: 
022226,001154:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT --
022227,001155: 
022228,001156:                                                                                                  #        SEE OUTPUT FROM LSR24.1 + R61LEM
022229,001157: 
022230,001158:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
022231,001159: 
022232,001160:                                                                                                  #        SET INPUT FOR LSR24.1
022233,001161: 
022234,001162:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
022235,001163: 
022236,001164:                                                                                                  #        SRCHOPT, ACMODFLG
022237,001165: 
022238,001166: 24,3206  E7,1733                                  EBANK=   DATAGOOD

022243,001171: 24,3211           00041                           ADRES    LOSCMFLG                              #  SURE DODES DOESN'T GO TO R21

022307,001235:                                                                                                  #  PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE R61LEM
022308,001236:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022309,001237: 
022310,001238:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO: 3               DATE: 4-11-67
022311,001239:                                                                                                  #        MOD BY: P. VOLANTE, SDC
022312,001240: 
022313,001241:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION --
022314,001242: 
022315,001243:                                                                                                  #        TO COMPUTE THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE OF THE LM TO ENABLE RR
022316,001244:                                                                                                  #        TRACKING OF THE CSM AND TO PERFORM THE MANEUVER TO THE PREFERRED

022516,001444:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME: RRLIMCHK
022517,001445: 
022518,001446:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
022519,001447: 
022520,001448:                                                                                                  #        RRLIMCHK CHECKS RR DESIRED GIMBAL ANGLES TO SEE IF THEY ARE WITHIN
022521,001449:                                                                                                  #        THE LIMITS OF THE CURRENT MODE.  INITIALLY THE DESIRED TRUNNION AND
022522,001450:                                                                                                  #        SHAFT ANGLES ARE STORED IN ITEMP1 AND ITEMP2.  THE CURRENT RR
022523,001451:                                                                                                  #        ANTENNAE MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED WHICH IS = 0 FOR
022524,001452:                                                                                                  #        MODE 1 AND =1 FOR MODE 2.
022525,001453: 
022526,001454:                                                                                                  #        MODE 1 -- THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
022527,001455:                                                                                                  #        BETWEEN -55 AND +55 DEGREES.  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF WITHIN LIMITS,
022528,001456:                                                                                                  #        THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN -70 AND +59 DEGREES.
022529,001457:                                                                                                  #        IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF IN LIMITS, RETURN TO L +3.
022530,001458: 
022531,001459:                                                                                                  #        MODE 2 -- THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
022532,001460:                                                                                                  #        BETWEEN -139 AND -25 DEGREES.  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF WITHIN
022533,001461:                                                                                                  #        LIMITS, THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN +125
022534,001462:                                                                                                  #        AND -125 (+235) DEGREES.  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF IN LIMITS, RETURN
022535,001463:                                                                                                  #        TO L +3.
022536,001464: 
022537,001465:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022538,001466: 
022539,001467:                                                                                                  #        L  TC  RLIMCHK (WITH INTERRUPT INHIBITED)
022540,001468:                                                                                                  #        L  +1  ADRES  T,S  (DESIRED TRUNNION ANGLE ADDRESS)
022541,001469: 
022542,001470:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022543,001471: 
022544,001472:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES, MODEA, MODEB (OR DESIRED TRUNNION AND SHAFT
022545,001473:                                                                                                  #        ANGLES ELSEWHERE IN CONSECUTIVE LOCATIONS -- UNSWITCHED ERASABLE OR
022546,001474:                                                                                                  #        CURRENT EBANK).
022547,001475: 
022548,001476:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:   MAGSUB
022549,001477: 
022550,001478:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED:  NONE
022551,001479: 
022552,001480:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS:  NONE
022553,001481: 
022554,001482:                                                                                                  #  EXIT:         L + 2   (EITHER OR BOTH ANGLES NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE)
022555,001483:                                                                                                  #                L + 3   (BOTH ANGLES WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE)
022556,001484: 
022557,001485:    4523           00006        RRLIMCHK           EXTEND                                         
022558,001486:    4524           50002                           INDEX    Q

022600,001528:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME: SETTRKF
022601,001529: 
022602,001530:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
022603,001531: 
022604,001532:                                                                                                  #        SETTRKF UPDATES THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP ON THE DSKY.
022605,001533:                                                                                                  #        INITIALLY THE LAMP TEST FLAG (IMODES33 BIT 1) IS CHECKED.
022606,001534:                                                                                                  #        IF A LAMP TEST IS IN PROGRESS, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L +1.
022607,001535:                                                                                                  #        IF NO LAMP TEST THE FOLLOWING IS CHECKED SEQUENTIALLY:
022608,001536:                                                                                                  #                1) RR CDU'S BEING ZEROED, RR CDU OK, AND RR NOT IN
022609,001537:                                                                                                  #                   AUTO MODE (RADMODES BITS 13, 7, 2).
022610,001538:                                                                                                  #                2) LR VEL DATA FAIL AND NO LR POS DATA (RADMODES BITS
022611,001539:                                                                                                  #                   8,5)
022612,001540:                                                                                                  #                3) NO RR DATA (RADMODES BIT 4)
022613,001541:                                                                                                  #        THE ABSENCE OF ALL THREE SIMULTANEOUSLY IN (1), THE PRESENCE OF BOTH
022614,001542:                                                                                                  #        IN (2), AND THE PRESENCE OF (3) RESULTS IN EITHER THE TRACKER FAIL
022615,001543:                                                                                                  #        LAMP (DSPTAB +11D BIT 8) BEING TURNED OFF OR IS LEFT OFF.  THEREFORE, THE
022616,001544:                                                                                                  #        TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURN ON IF:
022617,001545:                                                                                                  #                A) RR CDU FAILED WITH RR IN AUTO MODE AND RR CDU'S NOT BEING ZEROED
022618,001546:                                                                                                  #                B) N SAMPLES OF LR DATA COULD NOT BE TAKEN IN 2N TRIES WITH
022619,001547:                                                                                                  #                   EITHER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION
022620,001548:                                                                                                  #                C) N SAMPLES OF RR DATA COULD NOT BE OBTAINED FROM 2N TRIES
022621,001549:                                                                                                  #                   WITH EITHER THE AL
022622,001550: 
022623,001551:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022624,001552: 
022625,001553:                                                                                                  #        L       TC      SETTRKF
022626,001554: 
022627,001555:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:  IMODES33, RADMODES, DSPTAB +11D
022628,001556: 
022629,001557:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:  NONE
022630,001558: 
022631,001559:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED:  NONE
022632,001560: 
022633,001561:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS:  TRACKER FAIL LAMP
022634,001562: 
022635,001563:                                                                                                  #  EXIT:  L +1 (ALWAYS)
022636,001564: 
022637,001565:    4564           34753        SETTRKF            CAF      BIT1                                  #  NO ACTION IF DURING LAMP TEST
022638,001566:    4565           71303                           MASK     IMODES33                              
022639,001567:    4566           10000                           CCS      A                                     
022640,001568:    4567           00002                           TC       Q                                     
022641,001569: 
022642,001570:    4570           34744        RRTRKF             CA       BIT8                                  
022643,001571:    4571           54001                           TS       L                                     
022644,001572:

022672,001600:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME:  RRTURNON
022673,001601: 
022674,001602:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
022675,001603: 
022676,001604:                                                                                                  #        RRTURNON IS THE TURN-ON SEQUENCE WHICH, ALONG WTIH
022677,001605:                                                                                                  #        RRZEROSB, ZEROES THE CDU'S AND DETERMINES THE RR MODE.
022678,001606:                                                                                                  #        INITIALLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RRZEROSB FOR THE
022679,001607:                                                                                                  #        ACTUAL TURN-ON SEQUENCE.  UPON RETURN THE PROGRAM
022680,001608:                                                                                                  #        WAITS 1 SECOND BEFORE REMOVING THE TURN-ON FLAG
022681,001609:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT1) SO THE REPOSITION ROUTINE WON'T
022682,001610:                                                                                                  #        INITIATE PROGRAM ALARM 00501.  A CHECK IS THEN MADE
022683,001611:                                                                                                  #        TO SEE IF A PROGRAM IS USING THE RR (STATE BIT 7).  IF
022684,001612:                                                                                                  #        SO, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR SO THAT THE RR CDU
022685,001613:                                                                                                  #        FAIL FLAG (RADMODES BIT 7) CAN BE CHECKED BEFORE
022686,001614:                                                                                                  #        RETURNING TO THE WAITING PROGRAM.  IF NOT, THE PROGRAM EXITS
022687,001615:                                                                                                  #        TO TASKOVER.
022688,001616: 
022689,001617:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  WAITLIST TASK FROM RRAUTCHK IF THE RR POWER-ON AUTO
022690,001618:                                                                                                  #  BIT (CHAN 33 BIT 2) CHANGES TO 0 AND NO PROGRAM WAS USING 
022691,001619:                                                                                                  #  THE RR (STATE BIT 7).
022692,001620: 
022693,001621:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022694,001622: 
022695,001623:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES, STATE
022696,001624: 
022697,001625:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:  RRZEROSB, FIXDELAY, TASKOVER, ENDRADAR
022698,001626: 
022699,001627:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED:
022700,001628:                                                                                                  #        
022701,001629:                                                                                                  #        NONE
022702,001630: 
022703,001631:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS:  NONE (SEE RRZEROSB)
022704,001632: 
022705,001633:                                                                                                  #  EXIT:  TASKOVER, ENDRADAR (WAITING PROGRAM)
022706,001634: 
022707,001635: 24,3255                                           BANK     24                                    
022708,001636: 25,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S1                                 
022709,001637: 25,2000                                           BANK                                           
022710,001638: 
022711,001639: 25,2062  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
022712,001640: 25,2062                                           COUNT*   $$/RSUB

022721,001649:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME:  RRZEROSB
022722,001650: 
022723,001651:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
022724,001652: 
022725,001653:                                                                                                  #        RRZEROSB IS A CLOSED SUBROUTINE TO ZERO THE RR CDU'S,
022726,001654:                                                                                                  #        DETERMINE THE RR MODE, AND TURN ON THE TRACKER FAIL
022727,001655:                                                                                                  #        LAMP IF REQUIRED.  INITIALLY THE RR CDU ZERO BIT (CHAN 12
022728,001656:                                                                                                  #        BIT 1) IS SET.  FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT, THE LGC
022729,001657:                                                                                                  #        RR CDU COUNTERS (OPTY, OPTX) ARE SET = 0 AFTER 
022730,001658:                                                                                                  #        WHICH THE RR CDU ZERO DISCRETE (CHAN 12 BIT 1) IS
022731,001659:                                                                                                  #        REMOVED.  A 4 SECOND WAIT IS SET TO ALL THE RR CDU'S
022732,001660:                                                                                                  #        TO REPEAT THE ACTUAL TRUNNION AND SHAFT ANGLES.  THE
022733,001661:                                                                                                  #        RR CDU ZERO FLAG (RADMODES BIT 13) IS REMOVED.  THE
022734,001662:                                                                                                  #        CONTENTS OF OPTY IS THEN CHECKED TO SEE IF THE TRUNNION
022735,001663:                                                                                                  #        ANGLE IS LESS THAN 90 DEGREES.  IF NOT, BIT 12 OF
022736,001664:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES IS SET = 1 TO INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 2.
022737,001665:                                                                                                  #        IF LESS THAN 90 DEGREES, BIT 12 OF RADMODES IS SET = 0 TO
022738,001666:                                                                                                  #        INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 1.  SETTRKF IS THEN CALLED TO
022739,001667:                                                                                                  #        SEE IF THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP SHOULD BE TURNED ON.
022740,001668: 
022741,001669:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  L  TC  RRZEROSB  (FROM RRTURNON AND RRZERO)

022743,001671:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022744,001672: 
022745,001673:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES (BIT 13 SET), DSPTAB +11D
022746,001674:

022754,001682:

022798,001726:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME:  DORREPOS
022799,001727: 
022800,001728:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
022801,001729: 
022802,001730:                                                                                                  #        DORREPOS IS A SEQUENCE OF TASKS TO DRIVE THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
022803,001731:                                                                                                  #        TO A SAFE POSITION.  INIITALLY SETRRECR IS CALLED WHERE THE RR
022804,001732:                                                                                                  #        ERROR COUNTERS (CHAN 12 BIT 2) ARE ENABLED AND LASTYCMD
022805,001733:                                                                                                  #        AND LASTXCMD SET = 0 TO INDICATE THE DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE
022806,001734:                                                                                                  #        DESIRED STATE AND PRESENT STATE OF THE COMMANDS.  THE RR
022807,001735:                                                                                                  #        TURN-ON FLAG (RADMODES BIT 1) IS CHECKED AND IF NOT PRESENT,
022808,001736:                                                                                                  #        PROGRAM ALARM 00501 IS REQUESTED BEFORE CONTINUING.  IN EITHER
022809,001737:                                                                                                  #        CASE, FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT THE PROGRAM CHECKS THE CURRENT
022810,001738:                                                                                                  #        RR ANTENNA MODE (RADMODES BIT 12).  RRTONLY IS THEN CALLED
022811,001739:                                                                                                  #        TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO 180
022812,001740:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES IF IN MODE 2.  UPON RETURN, THE CURRENT RR ANTENNA
022813,001741:                                                                                                  #        MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS AGAIN CHECKED.  RRSONLY IS THEN
022814,001742:                                                                                                  #        CALLED TO DRIVE THE SHAFT ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO
022815,001743:                                                                                                  #        -90 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2.  IF DURING RRTONLY OR RRSONLY A
022816,001744:                                                                                                  #        REMODE HAS BEEN REQUESTED (RADMODES BIT 14), AND ALWAYS
022817,001745:                                                                                                  #        FOLLOWING COMPLETION OF RRSONLY, CONTROL IS TRANFERRED TO
022818,001746:                                                                                                  #        REPOSRPT.  HERE THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS 
022819,001747:                                                                                                  #        REMOVED.  A CHECK IS THEN MADE ON THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
022820,001748:                                                                                                  #        BIT 10).  IF PRESENT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO BEGDES.  IF NOT PRESENT
022821,001749:                                                                                                  #        INDICATING NO FURTHER ANTENNA CONTROL REQUIRED, THE RR ERROR
022822,001750:                                                                                                  #        COUNTER BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS REMOVED AND THE ROUTINE EXITS TO
022823,001751:                                                                                                  #        TASKOVER.
022824,001752: 
022825,001753:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022826,001754: 
022827,001755:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST CALL FROM RRGIMON IF TRUNNION AND SHAFT CDU ANGLES
022828,001756:                                                                                                  #        NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE.
022829,001757: 
022830,001758:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022831,001759: 
022832,001760:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES
022833,001761: 
022834,001762:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
022835,001763: 
022836,001764:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY, RRSONLY, BEGDES (EXIT)
022837,001765: 
022838,001766:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED:
022839,001767: 
022840,001768:                                                                                                  #        NONE
022841,001769:

022891,001819:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME:  REMODE
022892,001820: 
022893,001821:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022894,001822: 
022895,001823:                                                                                                  #        REMODE IS THE GENERAL REMODING SUBROUTINE.  IT DRIVES THE
022896,001824:                                                                                                  #        TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF THE CURRENT MODE IS MODE 1,
022897,001825:                                                                                                  #        180 DEGREES FOR MODE 2, THEN DRIVES THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45
022898,001826:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES, AND FINALLY DRIVES THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130 DEGREES,
022899,001827:                                                                                                  #        TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2, -50 DEGREES FOR MODE 1, BEFORE
022900,001828:                                                                                                  #        INITIATING 2-AXIS CONTROL.  ALL REMODING IS DONE WITH SINGLE
022901,001829:                                                                                                  #        AXIS ROTATIONS (RR1AXIS).  INITIALLY THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
022902,001830:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED.  CONTROL IS THEN TRANSFERRED TO
022903,001831:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY TO DRIVE THR TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1
022904,001832:                                                                                                  #        OR 180 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2.  RRSONLY IS THEN CALLED TO DRIVE
022905,001833:                                                                                                  #        THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45 DEGREES. THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
022906,001834:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED AGAIN.  CONTROL IS AGAIN
022907,001835:                                                                                                  #        TRANSFERRED TO RRTONLY TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130
022908,001836:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2 IF CURRENTLY IN MODE 1 OR TO
022909,001837:                                                                                                  #        -50 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2 TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 1.  RMODINV
022910,001838:                                                                                                  #        IS THEN CALLED TO SET RADMODES BIT 12 TO INDICATE THE NEW
022911,001839:                                                                                                  #        RR ANTENNA MODE.  THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14)
022912,001840:                                                                                                  #        IS REMOVED TO INDICATE THAT REMODING IS COMPLETE.  THE PROGRAM
022913,001841:                                                                                                  #        THEN EXITS TO STDESIG TO BEGIN 2-AXIS CONTROL.
022914,001842: 
022915,001843:                                                                                                  #  CALLIN SEQUENCE:
022916,001844: 
022917,001845:                                                                                                  #        FROM BEGDES WHEN REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) IS SET.
022918,001846:                                                                                                  #        THIS FLAG MAY BE SET IN RRDESSM AND RRDESNB IF RRLIMCHK
022919,001847:                                                                                                  #        DETERMINES THAT THE DESIRED ANGLES ARE WITHIN THE LIMITS OF THE
022920,001848:                                                                                                  #        OTHER MODE.
022921,001849: 
022922,001850:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INIITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022923,001851: 
022924,001852:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES
022925,001853: 
022926,001854:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
022927,001855: 
022928,001856:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY, RRSONL, RMODINV (ACTUALLY PART OF)
022929,001857: 
022930,001858:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED:
022931,001859: 
022932,001860:                                                                                                  #        NONE
022933,001861:

022989,001917:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAMES:        RRTONLY, RRSONLY
022990,001918: 
022991,001919:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
022992,001920: 
022993,001921:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE SUBROUTINES FOR DOING SINGLE AXIS
022994,001922:                                                                                                  #        RR MANEUVERS FOR REMODE AND REPOSITION.  IT DRIVES TO
022995,001923:                                                                                                  #        WITHIN 1 DEGREE.  INITIALLY, AT RR1AX2, THE REMODE AND REPOSITION
022996,001924:                                                                                                  #        FLAGS (RADMODES BITS 14, 11) ARE CHECKED.  IF BOTH EXIST,
022997,001925:                                                                                                  #        THE PROGRAM EXITS TO REPOSRPT (SEE DORREPOS).  THIS INDICATES
022998,001926:                                                                                                  #        THAT SOMEONE POSSIBLY REQUESTED A DESIGNATE (RADMODES BIT 10)
022999,001927:                                                                                                  #        WHICH REQUIRES A REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) AND THAT A
023000,001928:                                                                                                  #        REPOSITION IS IN PROGRESS (RADMODES BIT 11).  IF NONE
023001,001929:                                                                                                  #        OR ONLY ONE OF THE FLAGS EXIST, REMODE OR REPOSITION, MAGSUB
023002,001930:                                                                                                  #        IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE APPROPRIATE ANGLE IS WITHIN 1 DEGREE.  IF YES,
023003,001931:                                                                                                  #        CONTROL RETURNS TO THE CALLING ROUTINE.  IF NOT, CONTROL IS
023004,001932:                                                                                                  #        TRANSFERRED TO RROUT FOR SINGLE AXIS MANEUVERS WITH THE OTHER
023005,001933:                                                                                                  #        ANGLE SET = 0.  FOLLOWING A .5 SECOND WAIT, THE ABOVE PROCEDURE IS
023006,001934:                                                                                                  #        REPEATED.
023007,001935: 
023008,001936:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:     L-1     CAF     *ANGLE*         (DESIRED ANGLE SCALED PI)
023009,001937:                                                                                                  #                        L       TC      RRTONLY         (TRUNNION ONLY)
023010,001938:                                                                                                  #                        RRSONLY                         (SHAFT ONLY)
023011,001939:                                                                                                  #                        RRTONLY IS CALLED BY PREPOS29;
023012,001940:                                                                                                  #                        RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE CALLED BY DORREPOS AND REMODE
023013,001941: 
023014,001942:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023015,001943: 
023016,001944:                                                                                                  #        C(A) = DESIRED ANGLE, RADMODES
023017,001945: 
023018,001946:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
023019,001947:

023021,001949:

023023,001951:

023082,002010:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME:  RROUT
023083,002011: 
023084,002012:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
023085,002013: 
023086,002014:                                                                                                  #        RROUT RECEIVES RR GYRO COMMANDS IN TANG, TANG +1 IN RR
023087,002015:                                                                                                  #        ERROR COUNTER SCALING.  RROUT THEN LIMITS THEM AND
023088,002016:                                                                                                  #        GENERATES COMMANDS TO THE CDU TO ADJUST THE ERROR COUNTERS
023089,002017:                                                                                                  #        TO THE DESIRED VALUES.  INITIALLY MAGSUB CHECKS THE MAGNITUDE OF
023090,002018:                                                                                                  #        THE COMMAND (SHAFT ON 1ST PASS) TO SEE IF IT IS GREATER THAN
023091,002019:                                                                                                  #        384 PULSES.  IF NOT, CONTROL IS TRANFERRED TO RROUTLIM TO
023092,002020:                                                                                                  #        LIMIT THE COMMAND TO +384 OR -384 PULSES.  THE DIFFERENCE IS
023093,002021:                                                                                                  #        THEN CALCULATED BETWEEN THE DESIRED STATE AND TEH PRESENT STATE OF
023094,002022:                                                                                                  #        THE ERROR COUNTER AS RECORDED IN LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD.
023095,002023:                                                                                                  #        THE RESULT IS STORED IN OPTXCMD (1ST PASS) AND OPTYCMD (2ND
023096,002024:                                                                                                  #        PASS).  FOLLOWING THE SECOND PASS, FOR THE TRUNNION COMMAND, THE
023097,002025:                                                                                                  #        OCDUT AND OCDUS ERROR COUNTER DRIVE BITS (CHAN 14 BITS 12, 11)
023098,002026:                                                                                                  #        ARE SET.  THIS PROGRAM THEN EXITS TO THE CALLING PROGRAM.
023099,002027: 
023100,002028:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023101,002029:                                                                                                  #        
023102,002030:                                                                                                  #        L TC RROUT (WITH RUPT INHIBITED) RROUT IS CALLED BY
023103,002031:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY, RRSONLY, AND DODES

023105,002033:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQURIED:
023106,002034:

023108,002036:                                                                                                  #        (1ST PASS = 0), RR ERROR COUNTER ENAGLE SET (CHAN 12 BIT 2).
023109,002037: 
023110,002038:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
023111,002039:

023192,002120:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME:  RRDESSM
023193,002121: 
023194,002122:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
023195,002123: 
023196,002124:                                                                                                  #        THIS INTERPRETIVE ROUTINE WILL DESIGNATE, IF DESIRED ANGLES ARE
023197,002125:                                                                                                  #        WITHIN THE LIMITS OF EITHER MODE, TO A LINE-OF-SIGHT (LOS) VECTOR
023198,002126:                                                                                                  #        (HALF-UNIT) KNOWN WITH RESPECT TO THE STABLE MEMBER PRESENT
023199,002127:                                                                                                  #        ORIENTATION.  INITIALLY THE IMU CDU'S ARE READ AND CONTROL
023200,002128:                                                                                                  #        TRANSFERRED TO SMNB TO TRANSFORM THE LOS VECTOR FROM STABLE
023201,002129:                                                                                                  #        MEMBER TO NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES (SEE STG MEMO 699)
023202,002130:                                                                                                  #        RRANGLES IS THEN CALLED TO CALCULATE THE RR GIMBAL ANGLES,
023203,002131:                                                                                                  #        TRUNNION AND SHAFT, FOR BOT THE PRESENT AND ALTERNATE MODE.
023204,002132:                                                                                                  #        RRLIMCHK IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE
023205,002133:                                                                                                  #        PRESENT MODE ARE WITHIN LIMITS.  IF WITHIN LIMITS, THE RETUREN
023206,002134:                                                                                                  #        LOCATION IS INCREMENTED, INASMUCH AS NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS
023207,002135:                                                                                                  #        REQUIRED, BEFORE EXITING TO STARTDES.  IF NOT WITHIN THE LIMITS OF THE
023208,002136:                                                                                                  #        CURRENT MODE, TRYSWS IS CALLED.  FOLLOWING INVERTING OF THE RR
023209,002137:                                                                                                  #        ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 12), RRLIMCHK IS CALLED
023210,002138:                                                                                                  #        TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE ALTERNATE MODE ARE WITHIN
023211,002139:                                                                                                  #        LIMITS.  IF YES, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG IS AGAIN INVERTED,
023212,002140:                                                                                                  #        THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) SET, AND THE RETURN LOCATION
023213,002141:                                                                                                  #        INCREMENTED, TO INDICATE NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED, BEFORE
023214,002142:                                                                                                  #        EXITING TO STARTDES.  IF THESE ANGLES ARE NOT WITHIN LIMITS
023215,002143:                                                                                                  #        OF THE ALTERNATE MODE, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES
023216,002144:                                                                                                  #        BIT 12) IS INVERTED BEFORE RETURNING DIRECTLY TO THE CALLING PROGRAM
023217,002145:                                                                                                  #        TO INDICATE THAT A VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED.
023218,002146: 
023219,002147:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023220,002148: 
023221,002149:                                                                                                  #        L       STCALL  RRTARGET        (LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN SM COORDINATES)
023222,002150:                                                                                                  #        L+1     RRDESM
023223,002151:                                                                                                  #        L+2     BASIC                   (VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
023224,002152:                                                                                                  #        L+3     BASIC                   (NO VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
023225,002153: 
023226,002154:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023227,002155: 
023228,002156:                                                                                                  #        RRTARGET, RADMODES
023229,002157: 
023230,002158:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
023231,002159: 
023232,002160:                                                                                                  #        READCDUS, SMNB, RRANGLES, RRLIMCHK, TRYSWS (ACTUALLY
023233,002161:                                                                                                  #        PART OF), RMODINV
023234,002162: 
023235,002163:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED:
023236,002164: 
023237,002165:                                                                                                  #        NONE
023238,002166: 
023239,002167:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS:  NONE
023240,002168: 
023241,002169:                                                                                                  #  EXIT:  L+2 (NEITHER SET OF ANGLES ARE WITHIN LIMITS OF RELATED MODE)
023242,002170:                                                                                                  #  STARTDES (DESIGNATE POSSIBLE AT PRESENT VEHICLES ATTITUDE -- RETURNS
023243,002171:                                                                                                  #  TO L+3 FROM STARTDES)
023244,002172:

023282,002210:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME:  STARTDES
023283,002211: 
023284,002212:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
023285,002213: 
023286,002214:                                                                                                  #        STARTDES IS ENTERED WHEN WE ARE READY TO BEGIN DESIGNATION.
023287,002215:                                                                                                  #        BIT 14 OF RADMODES IS ALREADY SET IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED.
023288,002216:                                                                                                  #        AT THIS TIME, THE RR ANTENNA MAY BE IN A REPOSITON
023289,002217:                                                                                                  #        OPERATION.  IN THIS CASE, IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED IT MAY HAVE
023290,002218:                                                                                                  #        ALREADY BEGUN BUT IN ANY CASE THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
023291,002219:                                                                                                  #        OTHERWISE, THE REPOSITION WILL BE COMPLETED BEFORE 2-AXIS
023292,002220:                                                                                                  #        DESIGNATION BEGINS.  INITIALLY DESCOUNT IS SET = 60 TO INDICATE
023293,002221:                                                                                                  #        THAT 30 SECONDS WILL BE ALLOWED FOR THE RR DATA GOOD INBIT
023294,002222:                                                                                                  #        (CHAN 33 BIT 4) IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED (STATE BIT 5).  BIT 10
023295,002223:                                                                                                  #        OF RADMODES IS SET TO SHOW THAT A DESIGNATE IS REQUIRED.
023296,002224:                                                                                                  #        THE REPOSITON FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED.  IF SET,
023297,002225:                                                                                                  #        THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM (SEE RRDESSM
023298,002226:                                                                                                  #        AND RRDESNB).  THE PROGRAM WILL BEGIN DESIGNATING TO THE DESIRED
023299,002227:                                                                                                  #        ANGLES FOLLOWING THE REPOSITON OR REMODE IF ONE WAS
023300,002228:                                                                                                  #        REQUESTED.  IF THE REPOSITON FLAG IS NOT SET, SETRRECR IS CALLED
023301,002229:                                                                                                  #        WITH SETS THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2)
023302,002230:                                                                                                  #        AND SETS LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD = 0 TO INDICATE THE
023303,002231:                                                                                                  #        DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE PRESENT AND DESIRED STATE OF THE ERROR
023304,002232:                                                                                                  #        COUNTERS.  A 20 MILLISECOND WAITLIST CALL IS SET FOR BEGDES
023305,002233:                                                                                                  #        AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF TEH CALLING PROGRAM.
023306,002234: 
023307,002235:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023308,002236: 
023309,002237:                                                                                                  #        FROM RRDESSM AND RRDESNB WHEN ANGLES WITHIN LIMITS.
