023456,002384:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME:  BEGDES
023457,002385: 
023458,002386:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
023459,002387: 
023460,002388:                                                                                                  #        BEGDES CHECKS VARIOUS DESIGNATE REQUESTS AND REQUESTS THE
023461,002389:                                                                                                  #        ACTUAL RR DESIGNATION.  INITIALLY A CHECK IS MADE TO SEE IF A
023462,002390:                                                                                                  #        REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) IS REQUESTED OR IN PROGRESS.  IF SO,
023463,002391:                                                                                                  #        CONTROL IS TRANFERRED TO STDESIG AFTER ROUTINE REMODE IS
023464,002392:                                                                                                  #        EXECUTED.  IF NO REMODE, STDESIG IS IMMEDIATELY CALLED WHERE
023465,002393:                                                                                                  #        FIRST THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED.  IF
023466,002394:                                                                                                  #        PRESENT, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS REMOVED
023467,002395:                                                                                                  #        AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO RDBADEND.  IF THE REPOSITION
023468,002396:                                                                                                  #        FLAG IS NOT PRESET, THE CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
023469,002397:                                                                                                  #        BIT 15) IS CHECKED.  IF PRESENT, AN EXECUTIVE CALL IS IMMEDIATELY
023470,002398:                                                                                                  #        MADE FOR DODES AFTER WHICH A .5 SECOND WAIT IS INITIATED BEFORE
023471,002399:                                                                                                  #        REPEATING AT STDESIG.  IF THE RR SEARCH ROUTINE (LRS24.1) IS DESIGNATING
023472,002400:                                                                                                  #        TO A NEW POINT (NEWPTFLG SET) THE CURRENT DESIGNATE TASK IS TERMINATED.
023473,002401:                                                                                                  #        IF CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE IS NOT WANTED, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
023474,002402:                                                                                                  #        BIT 10) IS CHECKED.  IF NOT PRESENT, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR TO
023475,002403:                                                                                                  #        CHECK RR CDU FAIL BEFORE RETURNING TO THE CALLING PROGRAM.  IF DESIGNATE
023476,002404:                                                                                                  #        IS STILL REQUIRED, DESCOUNT IS CHECKED TO SEE IF THE 30 SECONDS HAS
023477,002405:                                                                                                  #        EXPIRED BEFORE RECEIVING THE RR DATA GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4)
023478,002406:                                                                                                  #        SIGNAL.  IF OUT OF TIME, PROGRAM ALARM 00503 IS REQUESTED, THE
023479,002407:                                                                                                  #        RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE AND RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE
023480,002408:                                                                                                  #        (CHAN 12 BITS 14,2) BITS REMOVED, AND THE DESIGNATE FLAG
023481,002409:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 10) REMOVED BEFORE EEXITING TO RDBADEND.  IF
023482,002410:                                                                                                  #        TIME HAS NOT EXPIRED, DESCOUNT IS DECREMENTED, THE
023483,002411:                                                                                                  #        EXECUTIVE CALL MADE FOR DODES, AND A .5 SECOND WAIT INITIATED
023484,002412:                                                                                                  #        BEFORE REPEATING THIS PROCEDURE AT STDESIG.
023485,002413: 
023486,002414:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023487,002415: 
023488,002416:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST CALL FROM STARTDES
023489,002417:                                                                                                  #        TCF BEGDES FROM DORREPOS
023490,002418:                                                                                                  #        TC STDESIG RETURNING, FROM REMODE
023491,002419: 
023492,002420:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023493,002421: 
023494,002422:                                                                                                  #        DESCOUNT, FINDVAC
023495,002423: 
023496,002424:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED:  DODES
023497,002425: 
023498,002426:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS:  PROGRAM ALARM 00503 (30 SECONDS HAVE EXPIRED) WITH NO RR DATA
023499,002427:                                                                                                  #  GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) RECEIVED WHEN LOCK-ON (STATE BIT 5) WAS REQUESTED.
023500,002428: 
023501,002429:                                                                                                  #  EXIT:         TASKOVER (SEARCH PATTERN DESIGNATING TO NEW POINT)
023502,002430:                                                                                                  #                ENDRADAR (NO DESIGNATE -- RADMODES BIT 10)
023503,002431:                                                                                                  #                RDBADEND (REPOSITION OR 30 SECONDS EXPIRED)
023504,002432: 
023505,002433: 25,2573           40110        BEGDES             CS       RADMODES

023551,002479:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME:  DODES
023552,002480: 
023553,002481:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
023554,002482: 
023555,002483:                                                                                                  #        DODES CALCULATES AND REQUESTS ISSUANCE OF RR GYRO TORQUE
023556,002484:                                                                                                  #        COMMANDS.  INITIALLY THE CURRENT RR CDU ANGLES ARE STORED AND
023557,002485:                                                                                                  #        THE LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR TRANSFORMED FROM STABLE MEMBER TO
023558,002486:                                                                                                  #        NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES VIA SMNB IF NECESSARY.  THE
023559,002487:                                                                                                  #        SHAFT AND TRUNNION COMMANDS ARE THEN CALCULATED AS FOLLOWS:
023560,002488:                                                                                                  #                + SHAFT = LOS . (COS(S), 0, -SIN(S))  (DOT PRODUCT)
023561,002489:                                                                                                  #                - TRUNNION = LOS . (SIN(T)SIN(S), COS(T), SIN(T)COS(S))
023562,002490:                                                                                                  #        THE SIGN OF THE SHAFT COMMAND IS THEN REVERSED IF IN MODE 2
023563,002491:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 12) BECAUSE A RELAY IN THE RR REVERSES THE 
023564,002492:                                                                                                  #        POLARITY OF THE COMMAND.  AT RRSCALUP EACH COMMAND IS
023565,002493:                                                                                                  #        SCALED AND IF EITHER, OR BOTH, OF THE COMMANDS IS GREATER THAN
023566,002494:                                                                                                  #        .5 DEGREES, MPAC +1 IS SET POSITIVE.  IF A CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE 
023567,002495:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 15) IS DESIRED AND THE SEARCH ROUTINE IS NOT OPERATING,
023568,002496:                                                                                                  #        THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS CLEARED AND RROUT
023569,002497:                                                                                                  #        CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION (RADMODES BIT 11)
023570,002498:                                                                                                  #        IS IN PROGRESS.  IF A CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE AND THE SEARCH ROUTINE IS
023571,002499:                                                                                                  #        OPERATING (SRCHOPT FLAT SET) THE TRACK ENABLE IS NOT CLEARED.  IF NO
023572,002500:                                                                                                  #        CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE AND BOTH COMMANDS ARE NOT LESS THAN .5 DEGREES AS
023573,002501:                                                                                                  #        INDICATED BY MPAC +1, THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS
023574,002502:                                                                                                  #        CLEARED AND RROUT CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITON
023575,002503:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN PROGRESS.  IF BOTH COMMANDS ARE LESS THAN .5
023576,002504:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES AS INDICATED BY MPAC+1, THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT
023577,002505:                                                                                                  #        (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS CLEARED AND RROUT CALLED TO PUT OUT THE
023578,002506:                                                                                                  #        COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN
023579,002507:                                                                                                  #        PROGRESS.  IF BOTH COMMANDS ARE LESS THAN .5 DEGREES, THE
023580,002508:                                                                                                  #        LOCK-ON FLAG (STATE BIT 5) IS CHECKED.  IF NOT PRESETN, THE
023581,002509:                                                                                                  #        DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS CLEARED, AND ENDOFJOB
023582,002510:                                                                                                  #        CALLED.  IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED, THE RR AUTO TRACKER (CHAN 12
023583,002511:                                                                                                  #        BIT 14) IS ENABLED FOLLOWED BY A CHECK OF THE RECEIPT OF THE
023584,002512:                                                                                                  #        RR DATA GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) SIGNAL.  IF RR DATA GOOD
023585,002513:                                                                                                  #        PRESENT, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS CLEARED,
023586,002514:                                                                                                  #        THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS CLEARED,
023587,002515:                                                                                                  #        AND ENDOFJOB CALLED.  IF RR DATA GOOD IS NOT PRESENT, RROUT
023588,002516:                                                                                                  #        IS CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION
023589,002517:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN PROGRESS AFTER WHICH THE JOB IS TERMINATED
023590,002518:                                                                                                  #        VIA ENDOFJOB.
023591,002519: 
023592,002520:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023593,002521: 
023594,002522:                                                                                                  #        EXECUTIVE CALL EVERY .5 SECONDS FROM BEGDES.
023595,002523: 
023596,002524:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023597,002525: 
023598,002526:                                                                                                  #        RRTARGET (HALF-UNIT LOS VECTOR IN EITHER SM OR NB COORDINATES),
023599,002527:                                                                                                  #        LOKONSW (STATE BIT 5), RRNBSW (STATE BIT 6), RADMODES
023600,002528: 
023601,002529:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
023602,002530: 
023603,002531:                                                                                                  #        READCDUS, SMNB, CDULOGIC, MAGSUB, RROUT

Page 548 

023605,002533: 
023606,002534:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED:
023607,002535: 
023608,002536:                                                                                                  #        NONE
023609,002537: 
023610,002538:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS:  NONE
023611,002539: 
023612,002540:                                                                                                  #  EXIT:  ENDOFJOB (ALWAYS)
023613,002541:

024219,003147:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME:  LPS20.1 VECTOR EXTRAPOLATION AND LOS COMPUTATION
024220,003148:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO. 2    BY J.D. COYNE   SDC     DATE 12-7-66
024221,003149: 
024222,003150:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRPIPTION:
024223,003151:                                                                                                  #        1)      EXTRAPOLATE THE LEM AND CSM VECTORS IN ACCORDANCE WITH THE TIME REFERRED TO IN CALLER + 1.
024224,003152:                                                                                                  #        2)      COMPUTES THE LOS VECTOR TO THE CSM, CONVERTS IT TO STABLE MEMBER COORDINATES AND STORES IT IN RRTARGET.
024225,003153:                                                                                                  #        3)      COMPUTES THE MAGNITUDE OF TEH LOS VECTOR AND STORES IT IN MLOSV
024226,003154: 
024227,003155:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:     CALL
024228,003156:                                                                                                  #                                LPS20.1
024229,003157: 
024230,003158:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
024231,003159:                                                                                                  #        LEMPREC, CSMPREC
024232,003160: 
024233,003161:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT:  RETURN TO CALLER + 2.
024234,003162: 
024235,003163:                                                                                                  #  ERROR EXITS:  NONE
024236,003164: 
024237,003165:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS:  NONE
024238,003166: 
024239,003167:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT:
024240,003168:                                                                                                  #        LOS VECTOR (HALF UNIT) IN SM COORDINATES STORED IN RRTARGET
024241,003169:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF TEH LOS VECTOR (METERS SCALED B-29) STORED IN MSLOV
024242,003170:                                                                                                  #        RRNBSW CLEARED.
024243,003171: 
024244,003172:                                                                                                  #  INITIALIZED ERASABLE
024245,003173:                                                                                                  #        TDEC1 MUST CONTAIN THE TIME FOR EXTRAPOLATION
024246,003174:                                                                                                  #        SEE ORBITAL INTEGRATION ROUTINE
024247,003175: 
024248,003176:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS:
024249,003177:                                                                                                  #        MPAC DESTROYED BY THE ROUTINE
024250,003178: 
024251,003179: 23,2314                                           BANK     23                                    
024252,003180: 24,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S                                  
024253,003181: 24,2000                                           BANK

Page 565 

024255,003183: 24,3255                                           COUNT*   $$/LPS20                              
024256,003184: 
024257,003185: 24,3255           43020        LPS20.1            STQ      BOFF                                  
024258,003186: 24,3256           01757                                    LS21X                                 
024259,003187: 24,3257           01343                                    LOSCMFLG                              #  LOSCMFLG = 0 MEANS NOT CALLED BY R21
024260,003188: 24,3260           51264                                    LMINT                                 #  SO CALL LEMCONIC TO GET LM STATE
024261,003189: 24,3261           77614                           BON                                            #  IF IN R21 AND ON LUNAR SURFACE
024262,003190: 24,3262           04307                                    SURFFLAG                              #  DON'T CALL LEMCONIC
024263,003191: 24,3263           51274                                    CSMINT                                
024264,003192: 24,3264           77624        LMINT              CALL                                           
024265,003193: 24,3265           27100                                    LEMCONIC                              #  EXTRAPOLATE LEM
024266,003194: 24,3266           77775                           VLOAD                                          
024267,003195: 24,3267           00001                                    RATT                                  
024268,003196: 24,3270           26352                           STOVL    LMPOS                                 #  SAVE LM POSITION B-29
024269,003197: 24,3271           00007                                    VATT                                  
024270,003198: 24,3272           16360                           STODL    LMVEL                                 #  SAVE LM VELOCITY B-7
024271,003199: 24,3273           00015                                    TAT

024348,003276:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME:  LRS22.1 (DATA READ SUBROUTINE 1)

024351,003279:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
024352,003280:                                                                                                  #        1)      READS RENDEZVOUS RADAR RANGE AND RANGE-RATE, TRUNNION AND SHAFT ANGLES, THREE CDU VALUES AND TIME.  CONVERTS THIS
024353,003281:                                                                                                  #                DATA AND LEAVES IT FOR THE MEASUREMENT INCORPORATION ROUTINE (LSR22.3).  CHECKS FOR THE RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE, FOR
024354,003282:                                                                                                  #                RR REPOSITION AND RR CDU FAIL

024366,003294:

024368,003296:                                                                                                  #        00001 -- ERROR EXIT 1 -- RR DATA NO GOOD (NO RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE OR RR CDU FAIL OR RR REPOSITION)

024572,003500:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME -- LSR22.3                               DATE -- 29 MAY 1967
024573,003501:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO 3                                             LOG SECTION -- P20-P25
024574,003502:                                                                                                  #  MOD. BY -- DANFORTH                                   ASSEMBLY LEMP20S REV 10
024575,003503: 
024576,003504:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
024577,003505:                                                                                                  #        THIS ROUTINE COMPUTES THE B-VECTORS ADN DELTA Q FOR EACH OF THE QUANTITIES MEASURED BY THE RENDEZVOUS
024578,003506:                                                                                                  #        RADAR.  (RANGE, RANGE RATE, SHAFT AND TRUNNION ANGLES).  THE ROUTINE CALLS THE INCORP1 AND INCORP2 ROUTINES
024579,003507:                                                                                                  #        WHICH COMPUTE THE DEVIATIONS AND CORRECT THE STATE VECTOR.
024580,003508: 
024581,003509:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
024582,003510:                                                                                                  #        THIS ROUTINE IS PART OF P20 RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION FOR THE LM COMPUTER ONLY.  THE ROUTINE IS ENTERED FROM
024583,003511:                                                                                                  #        R22 LEM ONLY AND RETURNS DIRECTLY TO R22LEM FOLLOWING SUCCESSFUL INCORPORATION OF MEASURED DATA.  IF THE
024584,003512:                                                                                                  #        COMPUTED STATE VECTOR DEVATIONS EXCEED THE MAXIMUM PERMITTED.  THE ROUTINE RETURNS TO R22LEM TO DISPLAY
024585,003513:                                                                                                  #        THE DEVIATIONS.  IF THE ASTRONAUT ACCEPTS THE DATA R22LEM RETURNS TO LSR22.3 TO INCORPORATE THE
024586,003514:                                                                                                  #        DEVIATIONS INTO THE STATE VECTOR.  IF THE ASTRONAUT REJECTS THE DEVIATIONS, NO MORE MEASUREMENTS ARE
024587,003515:                                                                                                  #        PROCESSED FOR THIS MARK, I.E.,  R22LEM GETS THE NEXT MARK.
024588,003516: 
024589,003517:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
024590,003518:                                                                                                  #        WLINIT          LGCUPDTE        INTEGRV         INCORP1         ARCTAN
024591,003519:                                                                                                  #        GETULC          RADARANG        INCORP2         NBSM            INTSTALL
024592,003520: 
024593,003521:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT:
024594,003522:                                                                                                  #        CORRECTED LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (PERMANENT)
024595,003523:                                                                                                  #        NUMBER OF MARKS INCORPORATED IN MARKCTR
024596,003524:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF POSITION DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP METERS B-29
024597,003525:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF VELOCITY DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP +2 M/CSEC B-7
024598,003526:                                                                                                  #        UPDATED W-MATRIX
024599,003527: 
024600,003528:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024601,003529:                                                                                                  #        LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS
024602,003530:                                                                                                  #        W-MATRIX
024603,003531:                                                                                                  #        MARK TIME IN MKTIME
024604,003532:                                                                                                  #        RADAR RANGE IN RM METERS B-29
024605,003533:                                                                                                  #                RANGE RATE IN RDOTM METERS/CSES B-7
024606,003534:                                                                                                  #                SHAFT ANGLE IN RRSHAFT REVS. B0
024607,003535:                                                                                                  #                TRUNNION ANGLE IN RRTRUN REVS. B0
024608,003536:                                                                                                  #        GIMBAL ANGLES   INNER IN AIG
024609,003537:                                                                                                  #                        MIDDLE IN AMG
024610,003538:                                                                                                  #                        OUTER IN ACG
024611,003539:                                                                                                  #        REFSMMAT
024612,003540:                                                                                                  #        RENDWFLG
024613,003541:                                                                                                  #        NOANGFLG
024614,003542:                                                                                                  #        VEHUPFLG
024615,003543: 
024616,003544:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS:
024617,003545:                                                                                                  #        PUSHLIST -- ALL
024618,003546:                                                                                                  #        MX, MY, MZ (VECTORS)

Page 575 

024620,003548:                                                                                                  #        ULC, RXZ, SINTHETA, LGRET, RDRET, BVECTOR, W.IND, X78T
024621,003549: 
024622,003550: 13,2207                                           BANK     13

025013,003941: 
025014,003942:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
025015,003943:                                                                                                  #        LSR22.4 IS THE ENTRY TO PERFORM LUNAR SURFACE NAVIGATION FOR THE LM
025016,003944:                                                                                                  #        COMPUTER ONLY.  THIS ROUTINE COMPUTES THE BE-VECTORS AND DELTA Q FOR RANGE
025017,003945:                                                                                                  #        AND RANGE RATE MEASURED BY THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
025018,003946: 
025019,003947:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
025020,003948:                                                                                                  #        INTSTALL        LGCUPDTE        INCORP1         RP-TO-R
025021,003949:                                                                                                  #        INTEGRV         GETULC          INCORP2
025022,003950:

025024,003952:                                                                                                  #        CORRECTED CSM STATE VECTOR (PERMANENT)
025025,003953:                                                                                                  #        NUMBER OF MARKS INCORPORATED IN MARKCTR

Page 583 

025027,003955:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF POSITION DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22 DISP METERS B-29
025028,003956:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF VELOCITY DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP +2 M/CSEC B-7
025029,003957:                                                                                                  #        UPDATED W-MATRIX
025030,003958: 
025031,003959:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
025032,003960:                                                                                                  #        LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS
025033,003961:                                                                                                  #        W-MATRIX

025035,003963:                                                                                                  #        RADAR RANGE IN RM METERS B-29
025036,003964:                                                                                                  #        RANGE RATE IN RDOTM METERS/CSEC B-7
025037,003965:                                                                                                  #        VEHUPFLG
025038,003966:

025237,004165:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME LRS24.1          RR SEARCH ROUTINE
025238,004166:                                                                                                  #  MCD NO. 0                     BY P. VOLANTE, SDC              DATE 1-15-67
025239,004167: 
025240,004168:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
025241,004169: 
025242,004170:                                                                                                  #  DRIVES THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR IN A HEXAGONAL SEARCH PATTERN ABOUT THE LOS TO THE CSM (COMPUTED FROM THE CSM AND LM
025243,004171:                                                                                                  #  STATE VECTORS) CHECKING FOR THE DATA GOOD DISCRETE AND MONITORING THE ANGLE BETWEEN THE RADAR BORESIGHT AND THE
025244,004172:                                                                                                  #  LM +Z AXIS.  IF THIS ANGLE EXCEEDS 30 DEGREES THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE IS CALLED TO PERFORM AN
025245,004173:                                                                                                  #  ATTITUDE MANEUVER.
025246,004174: 
025247,004175:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -- BANKCALL FOR LRS24.1
025248,004176:

025255,004183:                                                                                                  #        RRNB            BANKCALL

Page 594 

025492,004420:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME: R29     (RENDEZVOUS RADAR DESIGNATE DURING POWERED FLIGHT)
025493,004421:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO. 2     BY H. BLAIR-SMITH       JULY 2, 1968
025494,004422: 
025495,004423:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
025496,004424: 
025497,004425:                                                                                                  #        DESIGNATES THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR TOWARD THE COMPUTES LOS TO THE CSM, WITH THE CHIEF OBJECTIVE OF OBTAINING RANGE
025498,004426:                                                                                                  #        AND RANGE RATE DATA AT 2-SECOND INTERVALS FOR TRANSMISSION TO THE GROUND.  WHEN THE RR IS WITHIN .5 DEGREE OF
025499,004427:                                                                                                  #        THE COMPUTED LOS, TRACKING IS ENABLED, AND DESIGNATION CONTINUES UNTIL THE DATA-GOOD DISCRETE IS RECEIVED.  AT
025500,004428:                                                                                                  #        THAT POINT, DESIGNATION CEASES AND A RADAR-READING ROUTINE TAKES OVER, PREPARING A CONSISTENT SET OF DATA FOR
025501,004429:                                                                                                  #        DOWN TELEMETRY.  THE SET INCLUDES RANGE, RANGE RATE, MARK TIME, TWO RR CDU ANGLES, THREE IMUCDU ANGLES, AND AN
025502,004430:                                                                                                  #        INDICATOR WHICH IS 1 WHEN THE SET IS CONSISTENT AND 0 OTHERWISE.  THE INDICATOR IS IN TRKMKCNT.
025503,004431: 
025504,004432:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  BEGUN EVERY 2 SECONDS AS AN INTEGRAL PART OF SERVICER
025505,004433: 
025506,004434:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
025507,004435: 
025508,004436:                                                                                                  #        REMODE          RRPONLY
025509,004437:                                                                                                  #        UNIT            MPACVBUF
025510,004438:                                                                                                  #        QUICTRIG        AX*SR*T
025511,004439:                                                                                                  #        SPSIN           SPCOS
025512,004440:                                                                                                  #        SETRRECR        RROUT
025513,004441:                                                                                                  #        RRRDOT          RRRANGE
025514,004442: 
025515,004443:                                                                                                  #  EXIT:  TO NOR29NOW, IN SERVICER.
025516,004444: 
025517,004445:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT:  (ALL FOR DOWNLINK)
025518,004446: 
025519,004447:                                                                                                  #        RM              RDOTM           (RAW)
025520,004448:                                                                                                  #        AIG             AMG             
025521,004449:                                                                                                  #        AOG             TRKMKCNT        TRKMKCNT = 00001 IF SET IS CONSISTENT,
025522,004450:                                                                                                  #        TANGNB          TANGNB +1       OTHERWISE TRKMKCNT = 00000.
025523,004451:                                                                                                  #        MKTIME

Page 595 

025525,004453: 
025526,004454:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
025527,004455: 
025528,004456:                                                                                                  #        NOR29FLG        READRFLG                (TO 1 AND 0 BY FRESH START) (RESET NOR29FLG TO LET SERVICER RUN R29)
025529,004457:                                                                                                  #        PIPTIME         RADMODES (BIT 10)       (BIT SET TO 0 BY FRESH START)
025530,004458:                                                                                                  #        R(CSM)          V(CSM)
025531,004459:                                                                                                  #        R               V                       (PIPTIME THRU V BY AVE G IN SERVICER)
025532,004460:

Page 600 

025722,004650:                                                                                                  #  R29DODES:  RR DESIGNATION LOOP FOR R29
025723,004651: 
025724,004652:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE DOES MUCH THE SAME THING AS DODES, BUT A GREAT DEAL FASTER.  IT TAKES THE NON-UNITIZED LOS VECTOR
025725,004653:                                                                                                  #  IN STABLE MEMBER COORDINATES (LOSSM) AND A DELTA-LOS IN SM AXES (LOSVDT/4) WHICH IS 1/2 SEC TIMES LOS VELOCITY,
025726,004654:                                                                                                  #  AND DEVELOPS THE SHAFT AND TRUNNION COMMANDS USING SINGLE PRECISION AS MUCH AS POSSIBLE, AND INTERPRETIVE NOT AT
025727,004655:                                                                                                  #  ALL.  THE UNIT(LOSM + LOSVEL * 1 SEC) IS COMPUTED IN DP AND TRANSFORMED TO NAV BASE COORDINATES IN DOUBLE PRE-
025728,004656:                                                                                                  #  CISION (USING SP SINES AND COSINES OF CDU ANGLES), AND THE REST IS DONE IN SP.
025729,004657: 
025730,004658:                                                                                                  #  THE FUNCTIONAL DIFFERENCE IS THAT R29DODES ALWAYS CLEARS LOSCMFLG WHEN IT ENDS, AND IT STARTS UP THE R29READ
025731,004659:                                                                                                  #  TASK WHEN LOCK-ON IS ACHIEVED.
025732,004660: 
025733,004661: 32,2547                                           BANK     32                                    
025734,004662: 32,2000                                           SETLOC   F2DPS*32                              
025735,004663: 32,2000                                           BANK                                           
025736,004664: 
025737,004665: 32,2547                                           COUNT*   $$/R29                                
025738,004666: 32,2547  E3,1760                                  EBANK=   LOSVDT/4                              
025739,004667: 
025740,004668: 32,2547           34753        R29DODES           CA       ONE                                   
025741,004669: 32,2550           55107                           TS       TANG                                  #  INDICATE 1ST PASS THRU VECTOR LOOP.
025742,004670: 32,2551           34756                           CA       FIVE                                  
025743,004671: 
025744,004672: 32,2552           10000        R29DVBEG           CCS      A                                     #  COUNT DOWN BY TWO'S IN VECTOR LOOP.
025745,004673: 32,2553           54002                           TS       Q                                     
025746,004674: 32,2554           11107                           CCS      TANG                                  
025747,004675: 32,2555           12563                           TCF      R29DPAS1                              #  DO THIS ON 1ST PASS THRU LOOP.
025748,004676: 
025749,004677: 32,2556           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  (A "PASS" HERE MEANS 3 TIMES AROUND).
025750,004678: 32,2557           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
025751,004679: 32,2560           31761                           DCA      LOSVDT/4                              
025752,004680: 32,2561           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
025753,004681: 32,2562           21102                           DAS      LOSSM                                 #  ADVANCE LOS VECTOR 1/2 SECOND.
025754,004682: 
025755,004683: 32,2563           00006        R29DPAS1           EXTEND                                         
025756,004684: 32,2564           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
025757,004685: 32,2565           31102                           DCA      LOSSM                                 
025758,004686: 32,2566           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     #  MOVE CURRENT LOS (1ST PASS) OR LOS PRO-
025759,004687: 32,2567           52156                           DXCH     MPAC       +1                         #  JECTED 1/2 SEC AHEAD (2ND PASS).
025760,004688: 32,2570           11107                           CCS      TANG                                  
025761,004689: 32,2571           12577                           TCF      R29DVEND                              #  BUG OUT HERE IN 1ST PASS.
025762,004690: 
025763,004691: 32,2572           00006                           EXTEND                                         
025764,004692: 32,2573           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
025765,004693: 32,2574           31761                           DCA      LOSVDT/4                              
025766,004694: 32,2575           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
025767,004695: 32,2576           20156                           DAS      MPAC       +1                         #  PROJECT LOS 1 SECOND AHEAD (2ND PASS).
025768,004696: 
025769,004697: 32,2577           10002        R29DVEND           CCS      Q                                     
025770,004698: 32,2600           12552                           TCF      R29DVBEG                              #  BRANCH TO CONTINUE VECTOR LOOP.
025771,004699:

Page 601 

025773,004701:                                                                                                  #  UNITIZE AND TRANSFORM TO NAV BASE AXES THE PRESENT LOS (1ST PASS) OR THE 1-SEC PROJECTED LOS (2ND PASS).
025774,004702:
